stick: You can craft stick with or without crafting_table.
beef: You have to kill cow to get beef. You don't need sword to kill it.
cobblestone: You need wooden_pickaxe to mine cobblestone.
cooked_beef: You have to smelt beef with furnace.
log: You can mine log without any tool.
planks: You can craft planks without crafting_table.
raw_iron: You need a stone_pickaxe to mine raw_iron.
iron_ingot: You can get iron_ingot by smelting raw_iron with furnace.
furnace: You can craft furnace with crafting table.
white_bed: You can craft white_bed with crafting table.
white_wool: You have to kill sheep to get white_wool.
crafting_table: You can craft crafting_table. You don't need any tool.
stone_pickaxe: You can craft stone_pickaxe with crafting_table.
iron_pickaxe: You can craft iron_pickaxe with crafting_table.
wooden_pickaxe: You can craft wooden_pickaxe with crafting_table.
Here are some examples:
Example 1)
Task: {"cobblestone":3}
Context: You need wooden_pickaxe to mine cobblestone.
Then, you would answer:
await exploreAndMine(bot, 'cobblestone', 3, 'wooden_pickaxe');

Example 2)
Task: {"beef":2}
Context: You have to kill a cow to get beef.
Then, you would answer:
await exploreAndKill(bot, 'cow', 2);

Example 3)
Task: {"iron_sword":1}
Context: You have to craft it with crafting table.
Then, you would answer:
await craftItemWithCraftingTable(bot, 'iron_sword',1);

Example 4)
Task: {"iron_ingot":2}
Context: You have to smelt raw_iron to get iron_ingot.
Then, you would answer:
await smeltItemWithFurnace(bot, 'raw_iron', 2, 'planks');
